## https://github.com/twardoch/svgn/actions/runs/16057440442

The failing job is due to test assertions expecting uppercase hex colors (e.g., "#FF00FF"), but the code in convert_rgb_to_hex (see convert_colors.rs) outputs lowercase hex (e.g., "#ff00ff"). Your code currently does not force the output case unless the convertCase parameter is set.

**Solution:**  
There are two ways to fix this, but the most robust is to update your test cases to accept lowercase hex output (which matches the default plugin behavior). Alternatively, you can change the plugin to always output uppercase hex by default, but this might break other uses.

### Recommended Fix: Update Tests to Accept Lowercase Hex

Change the relevant test assertions in your test functions to expect lowercase hex values:

**In `svgn/src/plugins/convert_colors.rs`:**
- At lines 434, 435, 436, 429, 466, update "#FF00FF" to "#ff00ff" and "#7F64FF" to "#7f64ff".

**Examples:**  
Change:
```rust
assert_eq!(convert_rgb_to_hex("rgb(255, 0, 255)"), Some("#FF00FF".to_string()));
assert_eq!(document.root.attributes.get("stroke"), Some(&"#FF00FF".to_string()));
```
To:
```rust
assert_eq!(convert_rgb_to_hex("rgb(255, 0, 255)"), Some("#ff00ff".to_string()));
assert_eq!(document.root.attributes.get("stroke"), Some(&"#ff00ff".to_string()));
```

### Optional: Force Uppercase Output in Plugin

If you prefer uppercase hex output, add a `convertCase` config parameter in your tests or update the plugin to use uppercase output by default. For example, in your test parameters:
```rust
let params = json!({
    "convertCase": "upper"
});
```
And then expect uppercase output in your assertions.

---

**Summary:**  
Update your test expected values to match the default lowercase hex output, or configure/force the plugin to use uppercase hex values. This will resolve the failed assertions and align your tests with your codeâ€™s output.

- See code: [svgn/src/plugins/convert_colors.rs@6b53d02](https://github.com/twardoch/svgn/blob/6b53d02f544f032374c7974f3f4b747d7b97840b/svgn/src/plugins/convert_colors.rs)

## https://github.com/twardoch/svgn/actions/runs/16057442914

The job is failing due to a syntax error in the script tools/set-cargo-version.sh. The log shows:

syntax error at -e line 1, near "if ;"

This is caused by the use of an undefined variable $inws in the Perl one-liner at line 18:

perl -pi -e "s/^version = \"[0-9][^\"]*\"/version = \"$VERSION\"/ if $inws; if (/^\\[workspace\\.package\\]/) { $inws=1 } elsif (/^\\[/ && !/^\\[workspace\\.package\\]/) { $inws=0 }" "$CARGO_TOML"

In Bash, variables are not automatically defined in Perl code. You need to initialize $inws before using it. Update the Perl command as follows to avoid the syntax error:

perl -pi -e 'BEGIN { $inws=0 } s/^version = "[0-9][^"]*"/version = "'$VERSION'"/ if $inws; if (/^\[workspace\.package\]/) { $inws=1 } elsif (/^\[/ && !/^\[workspace\.package\]/) { $inws=0 }' "$CARGO_TOML"

This adds BEGIN { $inws=0 } to ensure $inws is defined before it is used. Update the script at tools/set-cargo-version.sh line 18 accordingly.

Reference:
- Failing job log: https://github.com/twardoch/svgn/actions/runs/16057442914/job/45315252497#step:3:12
- Script: tools/set-cargo-version.sh (ref: 6b53d02f544f032374c7974f3f4b747d7b97840b)
- Workflow: .github/workflows/release.yml (ref: 6b53d02f544f032374c7974f3f4b747d7b97840b)
